19	# Enable kernel RTC synchronization.

37	
38	# Specify the key used as password for chronyc.
39	commandkey 1
40	
41	# Generate command key if missing.
42	generatecommandkey
43	
44	# Disable logging of client accesses.
45	noclientlog
46	
47	# Send a message to syslog if a clock adjustment is larger than 0.5 seconds.
48	logchange 0.5
49	
50	logdir /var/log/chrony
51	#log measurements statistics tracking
52	
53	leapsecmode slew
54	maxslewrate 1000
55	smoothtime 400 0.001 leaponly
